		<script>
    function isValidHashTagMD(hashTag){
        return hashTag.indexOf("D[") != -1 && hashTag.indexOf("]") != -1;
    };

    function getMapFromHashTagMD(hashTag){
        var map = {};
        hashTag = hashTag.substring(hashTag.indexOf("[")+1,hashTag.indexOf("]"));
        if(hashTag != ""){
            var tokens = hashTag.split(",");
            var token = null,key = null,value = null,sepIndex = null;
            for(i=0,n=tokens.length;i<n;i++){
                try{
                    token = tokens[i];
                    sepIndex = token.indexOf(":");
                    key = token.substring(0,sepIndex);
                    value = token.substring(sepIndex+1,token.length);
                    map[key] = value;
                }catch(e){
                }
            }
        }
        return map;
    };

    function trackHashMelidata(){
        var hashTag = window.location.hash;
        if(hashTag != ''){
            if(isValidHashTagMD(hashTag)){
                var map = getMapFromHashTagMD(hashTag);
                if(map["F"]){//From
                    melidata("add", "event_data", {'from':'breadcumb'});
                }
            }
        }
    };
</script>

                    pagination: true
                });

                    promoSlider.on('select', function() {
                        if (promoSlider.page() == 1) {
                            promoSlider.pause();
                        }
                    });

                    // pausa rotador en click sobre flechas, circulos y banner
                    $(promoSlider.element).on('click', function() {
                        promoSlider.pause();
                    });
                }

                $("#convertionSlider ul").removeClass('carousel-mask');

                var animation = new home.Animation();
                animation.init();

                    e.preventDefault();

                    if( $(this).hasClass('selected') ) {

	window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
		// init the FB JS SDK
		FB.init({
			appId: '175268255910551',
			status: true,
			cookie: true,
			xfbml: true
		});

				document.getElementById('facebook').style.display = "inline";
			}
		});
	};

	(function(d, s, id) {
		var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
		if (d.getElementById(id)) return;
		js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
		js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/es_ES/all.js";
		fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
	}(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));

    function trackAndGotToApp(id, href) {
        if(id == 'android'){
            meli_ga('send', 'event', 'MOBILE-APP-ANDROID', 'DOWNLOAD-BANNER', 'HOME');
        } else {
            meli_ga('send', 'event', 'MOBILE-APP-IOS', 'DOWNLOAD-BANNER', 'HOME');
        }
    }

    var hash = document.location.hash.substring(1);
    if( hash != "WM" && hash != "CM" && hash != "MOVE_FROM_DEREMATE" ) {

        home.layerFreemiumSell = (function () {

            var layerSay = function layerSayF (eventname) {
                var event;
                if (window.CustomEvent) {
                    event = new CustomEvent(eventname);
                } else {
                    event = document.createEvent('Event');
                    event.initEvent(eventname, true, true);
                }
                window.dispatchEvent(event);
            };

            /**
             * setFreemiumFlag
             * @param e --> event object
             * @param this --> Layer '#freeSellLayer'
             * */
            var setFreemiumFlag = function setFreemiumFlagF (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var relocate = function() {
                    window.location.href = e.currentTarget.href; // relocate browser
                };

                // this reference to Layer
                this.hide(); // hide layer

                if (window.addEventListener) {
                    window.addEventListener('closedFreemiumLayer', relocate, false);
                } else {
                    window.attachEvent('onclosedFreemiumLayer', relocate);
                }
            };
            init = function () {
                var content = generateFreemiumSellLayerContent();
                var timestamp = new Date().getTime();

                // Insert phantom element before the Sell button,
                // to use as reference for the layer
                $('.nav-header-btn-pub').before('<div class="free-sell-layer-trigger"></div>');

                $('.free-sell-layer-trigger').layer({
                    content: content,
                    event: 'click',
                    classes: 'ch-box-lite free-sell-layer',
                    points: 'rt rb',
                    offset: '50 15',
                    width: meli.siteId === 'MLB' ? 265 : 240,
                    closable: 'button',
                    onHide: function () {
                        $.store.set('closedFreemiumLayer', timestamp);
                        layerSay('closedFreemiumLayer');
                    },
                    onShow: function () {
                        // save layer reference
                        var that = this;
                        $('#sellBtn a, .free-sell-layer a:not(.ch-close)').on('click', function(e) {
                            // call method with Layer reference how context
                            setFreemiumFlag.call(that, e);
                        });
                    }
                }).show();
            },

                    generateFreemiumSellLayerContent = function () {
                        return    '<a href=' + "http://www.mercadolibre.com.ar/publicar-gratis?referer=homes_sell_layer" + ' class="ch-layer-link"> <div class="ch-layer-content">' +
                                '<h2>' + "Vende productos usados gratis!" + '</h2>' +
                                '<p>' + "Sin pagar comisin por venta. "  + '<span class="ch-layer-clickable">' + "Ver ms" + '</span></p>' +
                                '<span class="ch-close"></span>' +
                                '</div> </a>';
                    };

            return {
                init: init
            }

        })();

        // Instance
        if ($('.lt-ie8').length == 0) {
            if ($.store.get('closedFreemiumLayer')) {
                var valueStore = $.store.get('closedFreemiumLayer');
                var now = new Date().getTime();
                var lastView = now;

                if (typeof valueStore !== 'undefined' && parseInt(valueStore)) {
                    lastView = parseInt(valueStore);
                } else {
                    lastView = 0;
                }

                var diffNow = now - lastView;

                if (diffNow > (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 90)) {
                    home.layerFreemiumSell.init();
                }
            } else {
                home.layerFreemiumSell.init();
            }
        }
    }
 }, function() { 
	// Improve the #nav-footer-access-content behavior by scrolling to
	// the bottom when users open this section
	(function toggleFooter(win, doc) {
	    var el = doc.getElementById('nav-footer-access-switch');
	    if (!win.addEventListener || !el) { return; }

	    function scrollTo(scrollDuration) {
	        var scrollInterval = setInterval(function () {
	            // stop animation when window is scrolled to bottom
	            if ((win.innerHeight + win.scrollY) >= doc.body.offsetHeight) {
	                clearInterval(scrollInterval);
	                // move scroll 20px each time
	            } else {
	                win.scrollBy(0, 20);
	            }
	        }, 15);
	    }

	    // User interaction
	    el.addEventListener('change', function (ev) {
	        if (!this.checked) {
	            setTimeout(function () {
	                scrollTo(400);
	            }, 200);
	        }
	    });
	}(window, document));

	(function appDownload() {
	    if ( false ){

            var appDownloadLink = document.getElementById('footer-applink');

            function trackEventAppDownloadAnalytics(os, pageId) {
                if (typeof meli_ga !== 'undefined') {
                    var osTrack = os.toUpperCase();
                    meli_ga('send', 'event', 'MOBILE-APP-' + osTrack, 'DOWNLOAD-FOOTER', pageId);
                }
            }

            function handleAppDownload(event) {
                var os = event.currentTarget.getAttribute('data-os'),
                    pageId = event.currentTarget.getAttribute('data-pageId');

                // track event in analytics
                trackEventAppDownloadAnalytics(os, pageId);
            }

            tiny.on(appDownloadLink, 'click', handleAppDownload);
            }
	}());
